SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Address], [t].[CartTotalPrice], [t].[IsApproved], [t].[IsCompleted], [t].[UserId], [c0].[Id], [c0].[CartId], [c0].[CartLinePrice], [c0].[ProductId], [c0].[Quantity]

    SELECT TOP(1) [c].[Id], [c].[Address], [c].[CartTotalPrice], [c].[IsApproved], [c].[IsCompleted], [c].[UserId]
    FROM [Carts] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[UserId] = @__userId_0 AND [c].[IsCompleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [CartLines] AS [c0] ON [t].[Id] = [c0].[CartId]
